"use client";

import { useState, useMemo, useEffect, Suspense } from "react";
import Link from "next/link";
import { useSearchParams } from "next/navigation";
import { MapPin, Star, CheckCircle, Search, Camera, Drama, Users, Lightbulb, Palette, Wrench, User, Mic, Shirt, Layers, Briefcase, Clapperboard, LayoutGrid, List, Monitor, Smartphone, Video, Aperture, ImageIcon } from "lucide-react";
import EmptyState from "@/components/EmptyState";
import { DEPT_KEYWORDS } from "@/lib/filmRoles";

const PAGE_SIZE = 24;

export type ServerCreator = {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  role: string;
  positions: string[];
  location: string;
  image: string;
  rating: number;
  reviews: number;
  dayRate: string;
  available: boolean;
  credits: string[];
  skills: string[];
  bio?: string;
  verified: boolean;
  isReal: true;
};

const platformTabs = [
  { id: "alle",   label: "Alle Bereiche" },
  { id: "film",   label: "🎬 Film" },
  { id: "social", label: "📱 Social Media" },
  { id: "photo",  label: "📷 Fotografie" },
];

const kategorien = [
  // Film
  { id: "alle",             label: "Alle",              icon: Users,        platform: "alle",   active: "bg-gold/15 border-gold/30 text-gold",                       hover: "hover:border-gold/40 hover:text-gold" },
  { id: "vor-der-kamera",   label: "Schauspieler",      icon: Drama,        platform: "film",   active: "bg-rose-500/15 border-rose-500/30 text-rose-400",           hover: "hover:border-rose-500/40 hover:text-rose-400" },
  { id: "statisten",        label: "Statisten",         icon: Users,        platform: "film",   active: "bg-sky-500/15 border-sky-500/30 text-sky-400",              hover: "hover:border-sky-500/40 hover:text-sky-400" },
  { id: "models",           label: "Models",            icon: User,         platform: "film",   active: "bg-pink-500/15 border-pink-500/30 text-pink-400",           hover: "hover:border-pink-500/40 hover:text-pink-400" },
  { id: "regie",            label: "Regie",             icon: Clapperboard, platform: "film",   active: "bg-purple-500/15 border-purple-500/30 text-purple-400",     hover: "hover:border-purple-500/40 hover:text-purple-400" },
  { id: "kamera",           label: "Kamera",            icon: Camera,       platform: "film",   active: "bg-blue-500/15 border-blue-500/30 text-blue-400",           hover: "hover:border-blue-500/40 hover:text-blue-400" },
  { id: "licht",            label: "Licht",             icon: Lightbulb,    platform: "film",   active: "bg-amber-500/15 border-amber-500/30 text-amber-400",        hover: "hover:border-amber-500/40 hover:text-amber-400" },
  { id: "grip",             label: "Grip",              icon: Wrench,       platform: "film",   active: "bg-slate-500/15 border-slate-500/30 text-slate-400",        hover: "hover:border-slate-500/40 hover:text-slate-400" },
  { id: "ton",              label: "Ton",               icon: Mic,          platform: "film",   active: "bg-teal-500/15 border-teal-500/30 text-teal-400",           hover: "hover:border-teal-500/40 hover:text-teal-400" },
  { id: "maske",            label: "Maske & Hair",      icon: Palette,      platform: "film",   active: "bg-fuchsia-500/15 border-fuchsia-500/30 text-fuchsia-400",  hover: "hover:border-fuchsia-500/40 hover:text-fuchsia-400" },
  { id: "kostuem",          label: "Kostüm",            icon: Shirt,        platform: "film",   active: "bg-orange-500/15 border-orange-500/30 text-orange-400",     hover: "hover:border-orange-500/40 hover:text-orange-400" },
  { id: "szenenbild",       label: "Szenenbild / Art",  icon: Layers,       platform: "film",   active: "bg-indigo-500/15 border-indigo-500/30 text-indigo-400",     hover: "hover:border-indigo-500/40 hover:text-indigo-400" },
  { id: "produktion",       label: "Produktion",        icon: Briefcase,    platform: "film",   active: "bg-emerald-500/15 border-emerald-500/30 text-emerald-400",  hover: "hover:border-emerald-500/40 hover:text-emerald-400" },
  { id: "post",             label: "Postproduktion",    icon: Monitor,      platform: "film",   active: "bg-blue-500/15 border-blue-500/30 text-blue-400",           hover: "hover:border-blue-500/40 hover:text-blue-400" },
  // Social Media
  { id: "content-creation", label: "Content Creation",  icon: Smartphone,   platform: "social", active: "bg-purple-500/15 border-purple-500/30 text-purple-400",     hover: "hover:border-purple-500/40 hover:text-purple-400" },
  { id: "social-video",     label: "Social Video",      icon: Video,        platform: "social", active: "bg-fuchsia-500/15 border-fuchsia-500/30 text-fuchsia-400",  hover: "hover:border-fuchsia-500/40 hover:text-fuchsia-400" },
  // Fotografie
  { id: "fotografie",       label: "Fotografie",        icon: Aperture,     platform: "photo",  active: "bg-cyan-500/15 border-cyan-500/30 text-cyan-400",           hover: "hover:border-cyan-500/40 hover:text-cyan-400" },
  { id: "foto-post",        label: "Foto-Post",         icon: ImageIcon,    platform: "photo",  active: "bg-lime-500/15 border-lime-500/30 text-lime-400",           hover: "hover:border-lime-500/40 hover:text-lime-400" },
];

// Keyword matching
const katMap: Record<string, string[]> = {
  "vor-der-kamera":   [...DEPT_KEYWORDS["vor-der-kamera"], "hauptdarsteller", "nebendarsteller", "schauspieler/in"],
  statisten:          ["statist", "komparse", "extra", "background"],
  models:             ["model", "talent", "sprecher"],
  regie:              DEPT_KEYWORDS.regie,
  kamera:             DEPT_KEYWORDS.kamera,
  licht:              DEPT_KEYWORDS.licht,
  grip:               DEPT_KEYWORDS.grip,
  ton:                DEPT_KEYWORDS.ton,
  maske:              DEPT_KEYWORDS.maske,
  kostuem:            DEPT_KEYWORDS.kostuem,
  szenenbild:         DEPT_KEYWORDS.szenenbild,
  produktion:         DEPT_KEYWORDS.produktion,
  post:               DEPT_KEYWORDS.post,
  "content-creation": DEPT_KEYWORDS["content-creation"],
  "social-video":     DEPT_KEYWORDS["social-video"],
  fotografie:         DEPT_KEYWORDS.fotografie,
  "foto-post":        DEPT_KEYWORDS["foto-post"],
};

// Platform keyword sets for platform-level filtering
const platformKeywords: Record<string, string[]> = {
  film:   Object.entries(DEPT_KEYWORDS).filter(([k]) =>
    ["vor-der-kamera","statisten","models","regie","kamera","licht","grip","ton","maske","kostuem","szenenbild","produktion","post"].includes(k)
  ).flatMap(([,v]) => v),
  social: [...DEPT_KEYWORDS["content-creation"], ...DEPT_KEYWORDS["social-video"]],
  photo:  [...DEPT_KEYWORDS.fotografie, ...DEPT_KEYWORDS["foto-post"]],
};

type AnyCreator = ServerCreator;

function getPositions(c: AnyCreator): string[] {
  if ("positions" in c && Array.isArray(c.positions) && c.positions.length > 0) return c.positions;
  return [c.role];
}

function CreatorsInner({ serverCreators }: { serverCreators: ServerCreator[] }) {
  const searchParams = useSearchParams();
  const validIds = new Set(kategorien.map((k) => k.id));
  const initialKat = searchParams.get("kategorie") ?? "alle";

  const [query, setQuery] = useState("");
  const [aktivePlatform, setAktivePlatform] = useState<string>(() => {
    const kat = validIds.has(initialKat) ? initialKat : "alle";
    if (kat === "alle") return "alle";
    const found = kategorien.find(k => k.id === kat);
    return found?.platform ?? "alle";
  });
  const [aktiveKat, setAktiveKat] = useState(() => validIds.has(initialKat) ? initialKat : "alle");

  // Sync filter when URL changes (e.g. from navbar dropdown)
  useEffect(() => {
    const kat = searchParams.get("kategorie") ?? "alle";
    const resolved = validIds.has(kat) ? kat : "alle";
    setAktiveKat(resolved);
    if (resolved !== "alle") {
      const found = kategorien.find(k => k.id === resolved);
      if (found) setAktivePlatform(found.platform);
    }
  // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
  }, [searchParams]);

  const [availableOnly, setAvailableOnly] = useState(false);
  const [verifiedOnly, setVerifiedOnly] = useState(false);
  const [locationFilter, setLocationFilter] = useState("");
  const [sortKey, setSortKey] = useState("featured");
  const [viewMode, setViewMode] = useState<"grid" | "list">("grid");
  const [visibleCount, setVisibleCount] = useState(PAGE_SIZE);

  // Kategorien visible for active platform tab
  const visibleKategorien = useMemo(() =>
    kategorien.filter(k => k.id === "alle" || aktivePlatform === "alle" || k.platform === aktivePlatform),
    [aktivePlatform]
  );

  const allCreators = useMemo(() => serverCreators, [serverCreators]);

  const filtered = useMemo(() => {
    let result = [...allCreators];

    if (query.trim()) {
      const q = query.toLowerCase();
      result = result.filter(c =>
        c.name.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
        getPositions(c).some(p => p.toLowerCase().includes(q)) ||
        c.role.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
        c.location.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
        c.skills.some(s => s.toLowerCase().includes(q))
      );
    }

    // Platform-level filter (when no specific kategorie selected)
    if (aktivePlatform !== "alle" && aktiveKat === "alle") {
      const keys = platformKeywords[aktivePlatform] ?? [];
      if (keys.length > 0) {
        result = result.filter(c => {
          const posMatch = getPositions(c).some(p => keys.some(k => p.toLowerCase().includes(k)));
          const roleMatch = keys.some(k => c.role.toLowerCase().includes(k));
          return posMatch || roleMatch;
        });
      }
    }

    if (aktiveKat !== "alle") {
      const keys = katMap[aktiveKat] ?? [];
      if (keys.length > 0) {
        result = result.filter(c => {
          const posMatch = getPositions(c).some(p => keys.some(k => p.toLowerCase().includes(k)));
          const roleMatch = keys.some(k => c.role.toLowerCase().includes(k));
          return posMatch || roleMatch;
        });
      }
    }

    if (availableOnly) result = result.filter(c => c.available);
    if (verifiedOnly) result = result.filter(c => c.verified);
    if (locationFilter.trim()) {
      const loc = locationFilter.toLowerCase();
      result = result.filter(c => c.location.toLowerCase().includes(loc));
    }
    if (sortKey === "rating") result.sort((a, b) => b.rating - a.rating);
    if (sortKey === "reviews") result.sort((a, b) => b.reviews - a.reviews);
    return result;
  }, [query, aktiveKat, aktivePlatform, availableOnly, verifiedOnly, locationFilter, sortKey, allCreators]);

  // Reset pagination when filters change
  useEffect(() => { setVisibleCount(PAGE_SIZE); }, [filtered]);

  return (
    <div className="pt-16 min-h-screen">

      {/* Header */}
      <div className="bg-bg-secondary border-b border-border py-10 px-4">
        <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto">
          <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-4 flex-wrap mb-6">
            <div>
              <h1 className="font-display text-4xl font-bold text-text-primary mb-2">Kreative & Profis</h1>
              <p className="text-text-secondary">
                {allCreators.length}+ Filmschaffende, Content Creator und Fotografen.
              </p>
            </div>
            <Link
              href="/profile"
              className="px-5 py-2.5 bg-gold text-bg-primary text-sm font-semibold rounded-lg hover:bg-gold-light transition-colors shrink-0"
            >
              Mein Profil bearbeiten
            </Link>
          </div>

          {/* Suche */}
          <div className="flex gap-2 max-w-2xl mb-5">
            <div className="flex-1 flex items-center gap-2 bg-bg-elevated border border-border rounded-lg px-3 focus-within:border-gold transition-colors">
              <Search size={16} className="text-text-muted" />
              <input
                type="text"
                value={query}
                onChange={(e) => setQuery(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="Name, Beruf, Fähigkeit oder Stadt..."
                className="bg-transparent border-none py-2.5 text-sm w-full focus:outline-none"
              />
              {query && <button onClick={() => setQuery("")} className="text-text-muted text-xs shrink-0">✕</button>}
            </div>
            <button className="px-4 py-2.5 bg-gold text-bg-primary text-sm font-semibold rounded-lg hover:bg-gold-light transition-colors">
              Suchen
            </button>
          </div>

          {/* Platform-Tabs */}
          <div className="flex gap-2 mb-4">
            {platformTabs.map(({ id, label }) => (
              <button
                key={id}
                onClick={() => { setAktivePlatform(id); setAktiveKat("alle"); }}
                className={`px-4 py-1.5 rounded-full text-sm font-semibold border transition-all ${
                  aktivePlatform === id
                    ? "bg-gold/15 border-gold/40 text-gold"
                    : "border-border text-text-muted hover:border-border-light hover:text-text-secondary"
                }`}
              >
                {label}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>

          {/* Kategorie-Chips */}
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
            {visibleKategorien.map(({ id, label, icon: Icon, active, hover }) => (
              <button
                key={id}
                onClick={() => setAktiveKat(id)}
                className={`flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-full text-xs font-medium transition-all border ${
                  aktiveKat === id ? active : `border-border text-text-secondary ${hover}`
                }`}
              >
                <Icon size={11} />
                {label}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Inhalt */}
      <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 py-8">
        <div className="flex gap-8">

          {/* Sidebar */}
          <aside className="hidden lg:block w-64 shrink-0">
            <div className="sticky top-20 p-5 bg-bg-secondary border border-border rounded-xl space-y-5">
              <h3 className="text-sm font-semibold text-text-primary">Filter</h3>

              <div className="pt-4 border-t border-border">
                <label className="text-xs uppercase tracking-widest text-text-muted font-semibold block mb-2">
                  Standort
                </label>
                <input
                  type="text"
                  placeholder="Stadt..."
                  value={locationFilter}
                  onChange={(e) => setLocationFilter(e.target.value)}
                  className="w-full text-xs py-2 px-2 bg-bg-elevated border border-border rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:border-gold transition-colors"
                />
              </div>

              <div className="pt-4 border-t border-border space-y-2.5">
                <label className="flex items-center gap-2 cursor-pointer">
                  <input type="checkbox" className="accent-gold" checked={availableOnly} onChange={(e) => setAvailableOnly(e.target.checked)} />
                  <span className="text-xs text-text-secondary">Nur verfügbare anzeigen</span>
                </label>
                <label className="flex items-center gap-2 cursor-pointer">
                  <input type="checkbox" className="accent-gold" checked={verifiedOnly} onChange={(e) => setVerifiedOnly(e.target.checked)} />
                  <span className="text-xs text-text-secondary flex items-center gap-1">
                    <CheckCircle size={11} className="text-success" /> Nur verifizierte
                  </span>
                </label>
              </div>
            </div>
          </aside>

          {/* Grid */}
          <div className="flex-1">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-5 gap-2 flex-wrap">
              <p className="text-sm text-text-muted">
                <span className="text-text-primary font-semibold">{filtered.length} {filtered.length !== 1 ? "Profile" : "Profil"}</span> gefunden
                {query && <span className="text-gold"> für &ldquo;{query}&rdquo;</span>}
                {filtered.length > visibleCount && <span className="text-text-muted"> · zeige {visibleCount}</span>}
              </p>
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 shrink-0">
                <div className="flex bg-bg-elevated border border-border rounded-lg overflow-hidden">
                  <button onClick={() => setViewMode("grid")} className={`p-2 transition-colors ${viewMode === "grid" ? "bg-gold text-bg-primary" : "text-text-muted hover:text-text-primary"}`}><LayoutGrid size={13} /></button>
                  <button onClick={() => setViewMode("list")} className={`p-2 transition-colors border-l border-border ${viewMode === "list" ? "bg-gold text-bg-primary" : "text-text-muted hover:text-text-primary"}`}><List size={13} /></button>
                </div>
                <select
                  value={sortKey}
                  onChange={(e) => setSortKey(e.target.value)}
                  className="text-xs py-2 px-3 bg-bg-secondary border border-border rounded-lg text-text-secondary focus:outline-none"
                >
                  <option value="featured">Empfohlen</option>
                  <option value="rating">Beste Bewertung</option>
                  <option value="reviews">Meiste Bewertungen</option>
                </select>
              </div>
            </div>

            {filtered.length === 0 && (
              <EmptyState
                icon={Users}
                title="Keine Profile gefunden"
                description="Versuche einen anderen Namen, eine andere Position oder Fähigkeit."
                action={{ label: "Filter zurücksetzen", onClick: () => { setQuery(""); setAktiveKat("alle"); setAvailableOnly(false); setVerifiedOnly(false); setLocationFilter(""); } }}
              />
            )}

            <div className={viewMode === "grid" ? "grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-3 gap-5" : "space-y-2"}>
              {filtered.slice(0, visibleCount).map((c) => {
                const displayPositions = getPositions(c);

                if (viewMode === "list") {
                  return (
                    <Link key={c.id} href={`/creators/${c.id}`}
                      className="card-hover group flex items-center gap-4 p-4 rounded-xl border border-border bg-bg-secondary hover:bg-bg-elevated transition-colors"
                    >
                      <div className="relative shrink-0">
                        {/* eslint-disable-next-line @next/next/no-img-element */}
                        <img src={c.image} alt={c.name} loading="lazy" decoding="async"
                          className="w-12 h-12 rounded-full object-cover border-2 border-border group-hover:border-gold transition-colors" />
                        <span className={`absolute -bottom-0.5 -right-0.5 w-3 h-3 rounded-full border-2 border-bg-secondary ${c.available ? "bg-success" : "bg-text-muted"}`} />
                      </div>
                      <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-0.5">
                          <h3 className="font-semibold text-text-primary text-sm">{c.name}</h3>
                          {c.verified && <CheckCircle size={12} className="text-success shrink-0" />}
                        </div>
                        <p className="text-xs text-gold truncate">{displayPositions.slice(0, 2).join(" · ")}</p>
                        <p className="text-xs text-text-muted flex items-center gap-1 mt-0.5"><MapPin size={10} /> {c.location}</p>
                      </div>
                      {c.skills.length > 0 && (
                        <div className="hidden sm:flex gap-1.5 shrink-0">
                          {c.skills.slice(0, 2).map((s) => (
                            <span key={s} className="text-[10px] px-2 py-0.5 bg-bg-elevated border border-border text-text-muted rounded-full">{s}</span>
                          ))}
                        </div>
                      )}
                      <span className={`text-xs font-semibold shrink-0 ${c.available ? "text-success" : "text-text-muted"}`}>
                        {c.available ? "Verfügbar" : "Gebucht"}
                      </span>
                    </Link>
                  );
                }

                return (
                  <Link
                    key={c.id}
                    href={`/creators/${c.id}`}
                    className="card-hover group rounded-xl border border-border bg-bg-secondary overflow-hidden block"
                  >
                    <div className="h-40 overflow-hidden bg-bg-elevated">
                      {/* eslint-disable-next-line @next/next/no-img-element */}
                      <img src={c.image} alt={c.name} loading="lazy" decoding="async"
                        className="w-full h-full object-cover group-hover:scale-105 transition-transform duration-300" />
                    </div>
                    <div className="p-5">
                      <div className="flex items-start gap-3 mb-3">
                        <div className="relative shrink-0 -mt-10">
                          {/* eslint-disable-next-line @next/next/no-img-element */}
                          <img src={c.image} alt={c.name} loading="lazy" decoding="async"
                            className="w-14 h-14 rounded-full object-cover border-2 border-bg-secondary shadow-lg" />
                          <span className={`absolute -bottom-0.5 -right-0.5 w-3.5 h-3.5 rounded-full border-2 border-bg-secondary ${c.available ? "bg-success" : "bg-text-muted"}`} />
                        </div>
                        <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
                          <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2 mb-1">
                            <h3 className="font-semibold text-text-primary text-sm leading-tight">{c.name}</h3>
                            {c.verified && <CheckCircle size={13} className="text-success shrink-0 mt-0.5" />}
                          </div>
                          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1 mb-1">
                            {displayPositions.slice(0, 2).map((p) => (
                              <span key={p} className="text-[11px] text-gold font-medium">{p}</span>
                            ))}
                            {displayPositions.length > 2 && (
                              <span className="text-[11px] text-text-muted">+{displayPositions.length - 2}</span>
                            )}
                          </div>
                          <p className="text-xs text-text-muted flex items-center gap-1">
                            <MapPin size={10} /> {c.location}
                          </p>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                      {"bio" in c && typeof c.bio === "string" && c.bio.length > 0 && (
                        <p className="text-xs text-text-muted leading-relaxed mb-3 line-clamp-2">{c.bio}</p>
                      )}
                      {c.skills.length > 0 && (
                        <div className="flex gap-1.5 flex-wrap mb-3">
                          {c.skills.slice(0, 3).map((s) => (
                            <span key={s} className="text-[10px] px-2 py-0.5 bg-bg-elevated border border-border text-text-muted rounded-full">{s}</span>
                          ))}
                        </div>
                      )}
                      <div className="flex items-center justify-between pt-3 border-t border-border">
                        <span className={`text-xs font-semibold ${c.available ? "text-success" : "text-text-muted"}`}>
                          {c.available ? "✓ Verfügbar" : "Gebucht"}
                        </span>
                        <span className="text-xs text-gold font-semibold group-hover:text-gold-light transition-colors">
                          Anfragen →
                        </span>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </Link>
                );
              })}
            </div>

            {filtered.length > visibleCount && (
              <div className="mt-8 text-center">
                <button
                  onClick={() => setVisibleCount(v => v + PAGE_SIZE)}
                  className="px-8 py-3 border border-border text-sm font-semibold text-text-secondary hover:border-gold hover:text-gold rounded-xl transition-all"
                >
                  Mehr laden · {filtered.length - visibleCount} weitere Profile
                </button>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export default function CreatorsContent({ serverCreators }: { serverCreators: ServerCreator[] }) {
  return (
    <Suspense fallback={<div className="pt-16 min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center"><div className="w-8 h-8 border-2 border-gold border-t-transparent rounded-full animate-spin" /></div>}>
      <CreatorsInner serverCreators={serverCreators} />
    </Suspense>
  );
}


================================================================
FILE: app/jobs/JobsContent.tsx
================================================================
"use client";

import { useState, useMemo, useEffect, useRef, Suspense } from "react";
import Link from "next/link";
import { useRouter, useSearchParams } from "next/navigation";
import { MapPin, Briefcase, Clock, Search, ChevronRight, Zap } from "lucide-react";
import EmptyState from "@/components/EmptyState";
import { FILM_DEPARTMENTS, DEPT_KEYWORDS } from "@/lib/filmRoles";

// Role filter tabs — Film + Social + Photo
const roleCategories = [
  "Alle Rollen",
  ...FILM_DEPARTMENTS.map((d) => d.label),
];

// Project/content types
const projectTypes = [
  "Alle Projekte",
  // Film
  "Spielfilm", "Kurzfilm", "Werbung", "Musikvideo", "TV / Serie", "Dokumentarfilm", "Corporate",
  // Social Media
  "Instagram / Reels", "TikTok", "YouTube", "UGC Content", "Brand Content",
  // Foto
  "Fashion Shooting", "Produkt-Shooting", "Event-Fotografie", "Portrait-Shooting", "Werbe-Fotografie",
];

// Platform tabs for jobs
const jobPlatformTabs = [
  { id: "alle",   label: "Alle" },
  { id: "film",   label: "🎬 Film" },
  { id: "social", label: "📱 Social Media" },
  { id: "photo",  label: "📷 Fotografie" },
];

// Which project types belong to which platform
const platformProjectTypes: Record<string, string[]> = {
  film:   ["Spielfilm", "Kurzfilm", "Werbung", "Musikvideo", "TV / Serie", "Dokumentarfilm", "Corporate"],
  social: ["Instagram / Reels", "TikTok", "YouTube", "UGC Content", "Brand Content"],
  photo:  ["Fashion Shooting", "Produkt-Shooting", "Event-Fotografie", "Portrait-Shooting", "Werbe-Fotografie"],
};
const PAGE_SIZE = 24;

type Job = {
  id: string; title: string; company?: string; projectType?: string;
  location: string; rate: string; union?: string; shootDates?: string;
  urgent?: boolean; tags: string[]; posted?: string;
  description?: string; isReal?: boolean;
};

function parseJobDescription(raw: string): { roleLabel?: string; company?: string; projectType?: string; shootDates?: string; urgent?: boolean; payType?: string; description: string } {
  const lines = raw.split("\n\n");
  if (lines.length < 2) return { description: raw };
  const metaLine = lines[0];
  const description = lines.slice(1).join("\n\n");
  const roleLabel = metaLine.match(/Rolle: ([^·\n]+)/)?.[1]?.trim();
  const company = metaLine.match(/Produktion: ([^·]+)/)?.[1]?.trim();
  const projectType = metaLine.match(/Typ: ([^·]+)/)?.[1]?.trim() ?? metaLine.match(/Projekttyp: ([^·]+)/)?.[1]?.trim();
  const shootDates = metaLine.match(/Drehtage: ([^·]+)/)?.[1]?.trim();
  const urgent = metaLine.includes("⚡ Dringend");
  const payType = metaLine.match(/Vergütung: ([^·]+)/)?.[1]?.trim();
  return { roleLabel, company, projectType, shootDates, urgent, payType, description };
}

function JobsInner({ serverJobs }: { serverJobs: Job[] }) {
  const router = useRouter();
  const searchParams = useSearchParams();

  const allJobs = useMemo(() => serverJobs, [serverJobs]);

  const [query, setQuery] = useState(() => searchParams.get("q") ?? "");
  const [activeRole, setActiveRole] = useState(() => searchParams.get("role") ?? "Alle Rollen");
  const [activePlatform, setActivePlatform] = useState("alle");

  // Sync filter when URL changes (e.g. from navbar dropdown)
  useEffect(() => {
    const role = searchParams.get("role");
    if (role) {
      setActiveRole(role);
      // auto-detect platform from role
      const socialRoles = ["Content Creation", "Social Video"];
      const photoRoles = ["Fotografie", "Foto-Post"];
      if (socialRoles.some(r => role.includes(r))) setActivePlatform("social");
      else if (photoRoles.some(r => role.includes(r))) setActivePlatform("photo");
    }
  // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
  }, [searchParams]);
  const [activeType, setActiveType] = useState(() => searchParams.get("type") ?? "Alle Projekte");
  const [urgentOnly, setUrgentOnly] = useState(() => searchParams.get("urgent") === "1");
  const [payTypeFilter, setPayTypeFilter] = useState(() => searchParams.get("pay") ?? "Alle");
  const [sortKey, setSortKey] = useState(() => searchParams.get("sort") ?? "newest");
  const [visibleCount, setVisibleCount] = useState(PAGE_SIZE);

  useEffect(() => {
    const timer = setTimeout(() => {
      const params = new URLSearchParams();
      if (query) params.set("q", query);
      if (activeRole !== "Alle Rollen") params.set("role", activeRole);
      if (activeType !== "Alle Projekte") params.set("type", activeType);
      if (urgentOnly) params.set("urgent", "1");
      if (payTypeFilter !== "Alle") params.set("pay", payTypeFilter);
      if (sortKey !== "newest") params.set("sort", sortKey);
      const qs = params.toString();
      router.replace(qs ? `/jobs?${qs}` : "/jobs", { scroll: false });
    }, 300);
    return () => clearTimeout(timer);
  }, [query, activeRole, activeType, urgentOnly, payTypeFilter, sortKey, router]);

  // Build roleKeywords from all FILM_DEPARTMENTS (incl. social/photo): label → DEPT_KEYWORDS entry
  const roleKeywords: Record<string, string[]> = Object.fromEntries(
    FILM_DEPARTMENTS.map((d) => [d.label, DEPT_KEYWORDS[d.id] ?? []])
  );

  // Visible project types based on active platform
  const visibleProjectTypes = useMemo(() => {
    if (activePlatform === "alle") return projectTypes;
    return ["Alle Projekte", ...(platformProjectTypes[activePlatform] ?? [])];
  }, [activePlatform]);

  const filtered = useMemo(() => {
    let result = [...allJobs];
    if (query.trim()) {
      const q = query.toLowerCase();
      result = result.filter((j) =>
        j.title.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
        (j.company ?? "").toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
        j.location.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
        j.tags.some((t) => t.toLowerCase().includes(q))
      );
    }
    if (activeRole !== "Alle Rollen") {
      const keys = roleKeywords[activeRole] ?? [];
      if (keys.length > 0) {
        result = result.filter((j) => {
          const titleMatch = keys.some((k) => j.title.toLowerCase().includes(k));
          if (titleMatch) return true;
          // Also check structured Rolle: field in description
          if (j.description) {
            const metaLine = j.description.split("\n\n")[0] ?? "";
            const roleMeta = metaLine.match(/Rolle: ([^·\n]+)/)?.[1]?.toLowerCase() ?? "";
            if (roleMeta && keys.some((k) => roleMeta.includes(k))) return true;
          }
          return false;
        });
      }
    }
    if (activeType !== "Alle Projekte") {
      result = result.filter((j) => j.projectType === activeType || (j.projectType ?? "").includes(activeType));
    }
    if (urgentOnly) result = result.filter((j) => j.urgent);
    if (payTypeFilter !== "Alle") {
      result = result.filter((j) => {
        if (!j.isReal) return true; // don't filter static placeholder jobs
        const parsed = parseJobDescription(j.description ?? "");
        return parsed.payType === payTypeFilter;
      });
    }
    if (sortKey === "rate-desc") result = [...result].sort((a, b) => parseInt(b.rate) - parseInt(a.rate));
    if (sortKey === "urgent") result = [...result].sort((a, b) => (b.urgent ? 1 : 0) - (a.urgent ? 1 : 0));
    return result;
  }, [allJobs, query, activeRole, activeType, urgentOnly, payTypeFilter, sortKey]);

  useEffect(() => { setVisibleCount(PAGE_SIZE); }, [filtered]);

  return (
    <div className="pt-16 min-h-screen">
      <div className="bg-bg-secondary border-b border-border py-10 px-4">
        <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto">
          <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-4 flex-wrap">
            <div>
              <h1 className="font-display text-4xl font-bold text-text-primary mb-2">Jobs & Ausschreibungen</h1>
              <p className="text-text-secondary">
                {allJobs.length} offene Stellen — Film, Social Media & Fotografie.
              </p>
            </div>
            <Link
              href="/inserat"
              className="px-5 py-2.5 bg-gold text-bg-primary text-sm font-semibold rounded-lg hover:bg-gold-light transition-colors flex items-center gap-2 shrink-0"
            >
              <Briefcase size={15} /> Job ausschreiben
            </Link>
          </div>

          <div className="flex gap-2 mt-6 max-w-3xl">
            <div className="flex-1 flex items-center gap-2 bg-bg-elevated border border-border rounded-lg px-3 focus-within:border-gold transition-colors">
              <Search size={16} className="text-text-muted" />
              <input
                type="text"
                value={query}
                onChange={(e) => setQuery(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="Rolle, Fähigkeit, Unternehmen oder Stichwort..."
                className="bg-transparent border-none py-2.5 text-sm w-full focus:outline-none"
              />
              {query && <button onClick={() => setQuery("")} className="text-text-muted text-xs">✕</button>}
            </div>
            <button className="px-4 py-2.5 bg-gold text-bg-primary text-sm font-semibold rounded-lg hover:bg-gold-light transition-colors shrink-0">
              Suchen
            </button>
          </div>

          {/* Platform tabs */}
          <div className="flex gap-2 mt-4 mb-3">
            {jobPlatformTabs.map(({ id, label }) => (
              <button key={id} onClick={() => { setActivePlatform(id); setActiveRole("Alle Rollen"); setActiveType("Alle Projekte"); }}
                className={`px-4 py-1.5 rounded-full text-sm font-semibold border transition-all ${
                  activePlatform === id ? "bg-gold/15 border-gold/40 text-gold" : "border-border text-text-muted hover:border-border-light hover:text-text-secondary"
                }`}>
                {label}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>

          {/* Role pills */}
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
            {roleCategories
              .filter(r => {
                if (activePlatform === "alle" || r === "Alle Rollen") return true;
                const dept = FILM_DEPARTMENTS.find(d => d.label === r);
                return dept?.platform === activePlatform;
              })
              .map((r) => (
                <button key={r} onClick={() => setActiveRole(r)}
                  className={`px-3 py-1.5 rounded-full text-xs font-medium transition-all border ${
                    activeRole === r ? "bg-gold text-bg-primary border-gold" : "border-border text-text-secondary hover:border-gold hover:text-gold"
                  }`}>
                  {r}
                </button>
              ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 py-8">
        <div className="flex gap-8">
          <aside className="hidden lg:block w-64 shrink-0">
            <div className="sticky top-20 space-y-4">
              <div className="p-5 bg-bg-secondary border border-border rounded-xl">
                <h3 className="text-sm font-semibold text-text-primary mb-4">Filter</h3>
                <div className="mb-5">
                  <label className="text-xs uppercase tracking-widest text-text-muted font-semibold block mb-2">Projekttyp</label>
                  <div className="space-y-1.5">
                    {visibleProjectTypes.map((t) => (
                      <label key={t} className="flex items-center gap-2 cursor-pointer group">
                        <input type="radio" name="projectType" className="accent-gold" checked={activeType === t} onChange={() => setActiveType(t)} />
                        <span className="text-xs text-text-secondary group-hover:text-text-primary transition-colors">{t}</span>
                      </label>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div className="pt-5 border-t border-border mb-5">
                  <label className="flex items-center gap-2 cursor-pointer">
                    <input type="checkbox" className="accent-gold" checked={urgentOnly} onChange={(e) => setUrgentOnly(e.target.checked)} />
                    <span className="text-xs text-text-secondary flex items-center gap-1"><Zap size={11} className="text-gold" /> Nur dringende Jobs</span>
                  </label>
                </div>
                <div className="pt-5 border-t border-border">
                  <label className="text-xs uppercase tracking-widest text-text-muted font-semibold block mb-2">Vergütung</label>
                  <div className="space-y-1.5">
                    {["Alle", "Paid", "Deferred", "Ehrenamtlich", "Expenses Only"].map((p) => (
                      <label key={p} className="flex items-center gap-2 cursor-pointer group">
                        <input type="radio" name="payType" className="accent-gold" checked={payTypeFilter === p} onChange={() => setPayTypeFilter(p)} />
                        <span className="text-xs text-text-secondary group-hover:text-text-primary transition-colors">{p}</span>
                      </label>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="p-4 bg-gold-subtle border border-gold/20 rounded-xl">
                <h4 className="text-xs font-semibold text-gold mb-2">Job ausschreiben</h4>
                <p className="text-xs text-text-muted leading-relaxed mb-3">Crew für dein Projekt gesucht? Jetzt kostenlos inserieren.</p>
                <Link href="/inserat" className="flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-2 bg-gold text-bg-primary text-xs font-semibold rounded-md w-full">
                  Job posten <ChevronRight size={12} />
                </Link>
              </div>
            </div>
          </aside>

          <div className="flex-1">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-5">
              <p className="text-sm text-text-muted">
                <span className="text-text-primary font-semibold">{filtered.length} {filtered.length !== 1 ? "Stellen" : "Stelle"}</span> gefunden
                {query && <span className="text-gold"> für &ldquo;{query}&rdquo;</span>}
              </p>
              <select value={sortKey} onChange={(e) => setSortKey(e.target.value)}
                className="text-xs py-2 px-3 bg-bg-secondary border border-border rounded-lg text-text-secondary">
                <option value="newest">Neueste zuerst</option>
                <option value="rate-desc">Gage (hoch → niedrig)</option>
                <option value="urgent">Dringend zuerst</option>
              </select>
            </div>

            {filtered.length === 0 && (
              <EmptyState icon={Briefcase} title="Keine Jobs gefunden"
                description="Versuche einen anderen Suchbegriff oder entferne aktive Filter."
                action={{ label: "Filter zurücksetzen", onClick: () => { setQuery(""); setActiveRole("Alle Rollen"); setActiveType("Alle Projekte"); setUrgentOnly(false); setPayTypeFilter("Alle"); } }} />
            )}

            <div className="space-y-3">
              {filtered.slice(0, visibleCount).map((job) => {

                const parsed = job.isReal ? parseJobDescription(job.description ?? "") : null;
                const roleLabel = parsed?.roleLabel;
                const company = parsed?.company ?? job.company;
                const projectType = parsed?.projectType ?? job.projectType;
                const shootDates = parsed?.shootDates ?? job.shootDates;
                const urgent = parsed?.urgent ?? job.urgent;

                return (
                  <Link key={job.id} href={`/jobs/${job.id}`}
                    className="card-hover group flex gap-4 p-5 rounded-xl border border-border bg-bg-secondary hover:bg-bg-elevated block">
                    <div className={`w-12 h-12 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 ${job.isReal ? "bg-emerald-500/10 border border-emerald-500/20" : "bg-gold/10 border border-gold/20"}`}>
                      <Briefcase size={20} className={job.isReal ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-gold"} />
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                      <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2 mb-1 flex-wrap">
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                          <h3 className="font-semibold text-text-primary">{job.title}</h3>
                          {urgent && (
                            <span className="px-2 py-0.5 bg-crimson/20 border border-crimson/40 text-crimson-light text-xs rounded font-semibold">Urgent</span>
                          )}
                          {job.isReal && (
                            <span className="px-2 py-0.5 bg-emerald-500/20 border border-emerald-500/30 text-emerald-400 text-xs rounded">Neu</span>
                          )}
                        </div>
                        <span className="text-gold font-semibold text-sm shrink-0">
                          {job.rate === "0 €/Tag" || job.rate === "0" ? "Nach Vereinbarung" : job.rate}
                        </span>
                      </div>
                      <p className="text-sm text-text-secondary mb-2 flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap">
                        {roleLabel && (
                          <span className="px-2 py-0.5 bg-sky-500/10 border border-sky-500/20 text-sky-400 text-xs rounded font-medium">{roleLabel}</span>
                        )}
                        {company}{company && projectType ? " · " : ""}{projectType}
                      </p>
                      <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-3">
                        {job.tags.map((t) => (
                          <span key={t} className="px-2.5 py-0.5 bg-bg-elevated text-text-muted text-xs rounded border border-border">{t}</span>
                        ))}
                        {"union" in job && job.union && (
                          <span className="px-2.5 py-0.5 bg-bg-elevated text-text-muted text-xs rounded border border-border">{job.union}</span>
                        )}
                      </div>
                      <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-4 text-xs text-text-muted">
                        <span className="flex items-center gap-1"><MapPin size={11} /> {job.location}</span>
                        {shootDates && <span className="flex items-center gap-1"><Clock size={11} /> {shootDates}</span>}
                        <span className="ml-auto text-text-muted">{job.posted}</span>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    <ChevronRight size={16} className="text-text-muted group-hover:text-gold transition-colors shrink-0 self-center" />
                  </Link>
                );
              })}
            </div>

            {visibleCount < filtered.length && (
              <div className="mt-6 text-center">
                <button
                  onClick={() => setVisibleCount((v) => v + PAGE_SIZE)}
                  className="px-6 py-2.5 bg-bg-secondary border border-border rounded-lg text-sm text-text-secondary hover:border-gold hover:text-gold transition-colors"
                >
                  Mehr laden · {filtered.length - visibleCount} weitere Jobs
                </button>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export default function JobsContent({ serverJobs }: { serverJobs: Job[] }) {
  return (
    <Suspense fallback={<div className="pt-16 min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center"><div className="w-8 h-8 border-2 border-gold border-t-transparent rounded-full animate-spin" /></div>}>
      <JobsInner serverJobs={serverJobs} />
    </Suspense>
  );
}

  Package, Car, Shirt, Camera, Lightbulb, Mic, Layers, Wrench,

  Smartphone, Video, Aperture,
} from "lucide-react";

// ─── Types ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

type LucideIcon = React.ElementType;

type CategoryItem = {
  id: string;
  label: string;
  icon: LucideIcon;
  type: "creator" | "job" | "prop" | "vehicle" | "location";
  category: string;
  color: string;
  bg: string;
};

type Group = { id: string; label: string; desc: string; color: string; border: string; items: CategoryItem[] };

// ─── Custom Role Dropdown ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

type RoleOption = { id: string; label: string; labelEn?: string };

function RoleDropdown({
  value,
  onChange,
  options,
  placeholder = "Rolle auswählen…",
}: {
  value: string;
  onChange: (val: string) => void;
  options: RoleOption[];
  placeholder?: string;
}) {
  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
  const ref = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handler = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      if (ref.current && !ref.current.contains(e.target as Node)) setOpen(false);
    };
    document.addEventListener("mousedown", handler);
    return () => document.removeEventListener("mousedown", handler);
  }, []);

  const selected = options.find((o) => o.label === value);

  return (
    <div ref={ref} className="relative">
      <button
        type="button"
        onClick={() => setOpen((o) => !o)}
        className={`w-full px-4 py-3 bg-bg-elevated border rounded-xl text-sm flex items-center justify-between transition-colors ${
          open ? "border-gold" : "border-border hover:border-border-hover"
        } ${selected ? "text-text-primary" : "text-text-muted"}`}
      >
        <span className="truncate">{selected ? selected.label : placeholder}</span>
        <ChevronDown
          size={15}
          className={`shrink-0 text-text-muted transition-transform duration-200 ml-2 ${open ? "rotate-180" : ""}`}
        />
      </button>
      {open && (
        <div className="absolute z-50 top-full mt-1.5 left-0 right-0 bg-bg-secondary border border-border rounded-xl shadow-2xl overflow-hidden max-h-60 overflow-y-auto">
          {options.map((opt) => (
            <button
              key={opt.id}
              type="button"
              onClick={() => { onChange(opt.label); setOpen(false); }}
              className={`w-full flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2.5 text-sm text-left transition-colors hover:bg-bg-elevated ${
                opt.label === value ? "text-gold bg-gold/5" : "text-text-secondary hover:text-text-primary"
              }`}
            >
              <span>{opt.label}</span>
              <span className="flex items-center gap-2 shrink-0 ml-2">
                {opt.labelEn && (
                  <span className="text-[11px] text-text-muted hidden sm:block">{opt.labelEn}</span>
                )}
                {opt.label === value && <CheckCircle size={13} className="text-gold" />}
              </span>
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
